href=\"#L2902\">2902</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2903\"><a href=\"#L2903\">2903</a></th><td>- also from 70, people who used triangle_count, it's now called</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2904\"><a href=\"#L2904\">2904</a></th><td>\u00a0 triangleCount.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2905\"><a href=\"#L2905\">2905</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2906\"><a href=\"#L2906\">2906</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2907\"><a href=\"#L2907\">2907</a></th><td>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2908\"><a href=\"#L2908\">2908</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2909\"><a href=\"#L2909\">2909</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2910\"><a href=\"#L2910\">2910</a></th><td>ABOUT REV 0070 - MEGABUCKET - 29 September 2004</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2911\"><a href=\"#L2911\">2911</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2912\"><a href=\"#L2912\">2912</a></th><td>YOUR CODE WILL ALMOST CERTAINLY BREAK IN THIS RELEASE, READ THE</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2913\"><a href=\"#L2913\">2913</a></th><td>\"MAJOR CHANGES\" SECTION BELOW TO SEE HOW TO FIX IT. this is one of the</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2914\"><a href=\"#L2914\">2914</a></th><td>most major releases to date in terms of things that have been changed,</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2915\"><a href=\"#L2915\">2915</a></th><td>fixed, or revised. unfortunately, there will still be api changes</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2916\"><a href=\"#L2916\">2916</a></th><td>before beta. if you don't want to deal with your code breaking, then</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2917\"><a href=\"#L2917\">2917</a></th><td>wait until the beta. </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2918\"><a href=\"#L2918\">2918</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2919\"><a href=\"#L2919\">2919</a></th><td>as of this release, we're also returning to more truly \"alpha\" status</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2920\"><a href=\"#L2920\">2920</a></th><td>for releases. from 70 until beta, releases will happen more frequently</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2921\"><a href=\"#L2921\">2921</a></th><td>(hopefully) and increment more quickly. however, we won't be</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2922\"><a href=\"#L2922\">2922</a></th><td>announcing a new release to the greater public until beta, at which</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2923\"><a href=\"#L2923\">2923</a></th><td>time we'll be done breaking everyone's code. more details here:</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2924\"><a href=\"#L2924\">2924</a></th><td>http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=Collaboration;action=display;num=1096489132</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2925\"><a href=\"#L2925\">2925</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2926\"><a href=\"#L2926\">2926</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2927\"><a href=\"#L2927\">2927</a></th><td>major changes: (things that break your code) </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2928\"><a href=\"#L2928\">2928</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2929\"><a href=\"#L2929\">2929</a></th><td>- if you have a program that uses \"void draw()\" to draw a static</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2930\"><a href=\"#L2930\">2930</a></th><td>\u00a0 image, you need to add the line \"noLoop()\" to setup or to the first</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2931\"><a href=\"#L2931\">2931</a></th><td>\u00a0 line of the draw method itself.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2932\"><a href=\"#L2932\">2932</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2933\"><a href=\"#L2933\">2933</a></th><td>- for any programs that use \"void loop()\" you need to change its name</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2934\"><a href=\"#L2934\">2934</a></th><td>\u00a0 to \"void draw()\". </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2935\"><a href=\"#L2935\">2935</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2936\"><a href=\"#L2936\">2936</a></th><td>- BImage, BFont, BGraphics, etc are all PImage, PFont, PGraphics.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2937\"><a href=\"#L2937\">2937</a></th><td>\u00a0 you'll need to rename them in your program.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2938\"><a href=\"#L2938\">2938</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2939\"><a href=\"#L2939\">2939</a></th><td>- libraries will almost certainly need to be rewritten for this</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2940\"><a href=\"#L2940\">2940</a></th><td>\u00a0 release. we're working with amit on an update to sonia and several</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2941\"><a href=\"#L2941\">2941</a></th><td>\u00a0 other libraries will be included in future releases.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2942\"><a href=\"#L2942\">2942</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2943\"><a href=\"#L2943\">2943</a></th><td>- mouse and key events are now properly queued, meaning that functions</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2944\"><a href=\"#L2944\">2944</a></th><td>\u00a0 like mousePressed() and keyPressed() will be called at the *end* of</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2945\"><a href=\"#L2945\">2945</a></th><td>\u00a0 your draw() method. this means that you can \"draw\" inside of those</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2946\"><a href=\"#L2946\">2946</a></th><td>\u00a0 methods, just note that it'll happen after all other drawing.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2947\"><a href=\"#L2947\">2947</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=Syntax;action=display;num=1079555200;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2948\"><a href=\"#L2948\">2948</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2949\"><a href=\"#L2949\">2949</a></th><td>- CENTER_DIAMETER has become CENTER</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2950\"><a href=\"#L2950\">2950</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2951\"><a href=\"#L2951\">2951</a></th><td>- replicate() in PImage is now called copy(). other changes in PImage</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2952\"><a href=\"#L2952\">2952</a></th><td>\u00a0 as well, see the ref: http://processing.org/reference/PImage.html</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2953\"><a href=\"#L2953\">2953</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2954\"><a href=\"#L2954\">2954</a></th><td>- curveSegments and bezierSegments are now called curveDetail and </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2955\"><a href=\"#L2955\">2955</a></th><td>\u00a0 bezierDetail.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2956\"><a href=\"#L2956\">2956</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2957\"><a href=\"#L2957\">2957</a></th><td>- net, serial, and video are completely different. see the libraries</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2958\"><a href=\"#L2958\">2958</a></th><td>\u00a0 reference: http://processing.org/reference/libraries/index.html</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2959\"><a href=\"#L2959\">2959</a></th><td>\u00a0 their examples have also been updated.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2960\"><a href=\"#L2960\">2960</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2961\"><a href=\"#L2961\">2961</a></th><td>- quicktime is no longer required to be installed on windows</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2962\"><a href=\"#L2962\">2962</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2963\"><a href=\"#L2963\">2963</a></th><td>- the 'fonts' folder has been removed. these were old (had no special</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2964\"><a href=\"#L2964\">2964</a></th><td>\u00a0 characters like umlauts and whatnot) and of questionable copyright</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2965\"><a href=\"#L2965\">2965</a></th><td>\u00a0 status, so we took them out. you can create fonts to your heart's</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2966\"><a href=\"#L2966\">2966</a></th><td>\u00a0 content using the \"Create Font\" option.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2967\"><a href=\"#L2967\">2967</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2968\"><a href=\"#L2968\">2968</a></th><td>- history has been (temporarily?) removed. in the meantime under the</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2969\"><a href=\"#L2969\">2969</a></th><td>\u00a0 \"Tools\" menu is an option named \"Archive Sketch\" which will zip up</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2970\"><a href=\"#L2970\">2970</a></th><td>\u00a0 the contents of the current sketch folder into a numbered archive.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2971\"><a href=\"#L2971\">2971</a></th><td>\u00a0 the numbers will automatically increment yoursketch-001.zip,</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2972\"><a href=\"#L2972\">2972</a></th><td>\u00a0 yoursketch-002.zip etc.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2973\"><a href=\"#L2973\">2973</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2974\"><a href=\"#L2974\">2974</a></th><td>- key events for things like arrow and whatnot should use 'keyCode'</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2975\"><a href=\"#L2975\">2975</a></th><td>\u00a0 instead of 'key'. so </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2976\"><a href=\"#L2976\">2976</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096304533;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2977\"><a href=\"#L2977\">2977</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096304779;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2978\"><a href=\"#L2978\">2978</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2979\"><a href=\"#L2979\">2979</a></th><td>- the sizing/spacing of text() has changed! a combination of small</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2980\"><a href=\"#L2980\">2980</a></th><td>\u00a0 bugs inside text() and the \"Create Font\" tool meant that text was</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2981\"><a href=\"#L2981\">2981</a></th><td>\u00a0 not sized properly. it's now been tweaked to more closely resemble</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2982\"><a href=\"#L2982\">2982</a></th><td>\u00a0 the sizing used by the platform. for\u00a0 instance, 48 point type of a</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2983\"><a href=\"#L2983\">2983</a></th><td>\u00a0 font in illustrator looks like 48 point type of the same font in</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2984\"><a href=\"#L2984\">2984</a></th><td>\u00a0 processing. </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2985\"><a href=\"#L2985\">2985</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2986\"><a href=\"#L2986\">2986</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2987\"><a href=\"#L2987\">2987</a></th><td>additions: </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2988\"><a href=\"#L2988\">2988</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2989\"><a href=\"#L2989\">2989</a></th><td>- hex(), binary(), unhex(), and unbinary() functions to make your</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2990\"><a href=\"#L2990\">2990</a></th><td>\u00a0 geeky debugging sessions that much happier. </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2991\"><a href=\"#L2991\">2991</a></th><td>\u00a0 color c = #ffcc00;</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2992\"><a href=\"#L2992\">2992</a></th><td>\u00a0 println(hex(c));</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2993\"><a href=\"#L2993\">2993</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2994\"><a href=\"#L2994\">2994</a></th><td>- support for text in a box: text(String text, x, y, width, height);</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2995\"><a href=\"#L2995\">2995</a></th><td>\u00a0 this is like the text box in adobe illustrator or programs like </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2996\"><a href=\"#L2996\">2996</a></th><td>\u00a0 that, note that the x, y where it starts will be the top of the</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2997\"><a href=\"#L2997\">2997</a></th><td>\u00a0 line of text, not the baseline of the text as is the case for</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2998\"><a href=\"#L2998\">2998</a></th><td>\u00a0 the other text() functions.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L2999\"><a href=\"#L2999\">2999</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3000\"><a href=\"#L3000\">3000</a></th><td>- operators for int(), string(), char(), and other basic types.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3001\"><a href=\"#L3001\">3001</a></th><td>\u00a0 String s = \"10.2\";</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3002\"><a href=\"#L3002\">3002</a></th><td>\u00a0 float f = float(s);</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3003\"><a href=\"#L3003\">3003</a></th><td>\u00a0 making it simpler to do conversions between types.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3004\"><a href=\"#L3004\">3004</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3005\"><a href=\"#L3005\">3005</a></th><td>- these operators also work on arrays:</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3006\"><a href=\"#L3006\">3006</a></th><td>\u00a0 String s[] = { \"10.2\", \"3.2\" };</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3007\"><a href=\"#L3007\">3007</a></th><td>\u00a0 float f[] = float(s);</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3008\"><a href=\"#L3008\">3008</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3009\"><a href=\"#L3009\">3009</a></th><td>- looping can be turned on/off via loop() and noLoop(). the default is</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3010\"><a href=\"#L3010\">3010</a></th><td>\u00a0 that loop() is in use. there's also a redraw() function that you can</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3011\"><a href=\"#L3011\">3011</a></th><td>\u00a0 use in noLoop() mode which lets you redraw the screen once (i.e. if</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3012\"><a href=\"#L3012\">3012</a></th><td>\u00a0 you want to update after a mouse event)</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3013\"><a href=\"#L3013\">3013</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3014\"><a href=\"#L3014\">3014</a></th><td>- multiple files! you can create new tabs that store separate classes</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3015\"><a href=\"#L3015\">3015</a></th><td>\u00a0 and pieces of code. how happy. however, the tabs are only separators</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3016\"><a href=\"#L3016\">3016</a></th><td>\u00a0 for your code.. the code is all still added to the main class (the</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3017\"><a href=\"#L3017\">3017</a></th><td>\u00a0 first tab) the same way as if the code had appeared all jammed into</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3018\"><a href=\"#L3018\">3018</a></th><td>\u00a0 that first file. </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3019\"><a href=\"#L3019\">3019</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3020\"><a href=\"#L3020\">3020</a></th><td>- for advanced users, additional tabs can be java files, which, unlike</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3021\"><a href=\"#L3021\">3021</a></th><td>\u00a0 the tabs described above, will *not* be embedded into the main</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3022\"><a href=\"#L3022\">3022</a></th><td>\u00a0 applet class. to create\u00a0 a java file, include \".java\" at the end of</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3023\"><a href=\"#L3023\">3023</a></th><td>\u00a0 the new file's name when creating the new tab. also note, however,</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3024\"><a href=\"#L3024\">3024</a></th><td>\u00a0 that the java files will not go through the preprocessor, meaning</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3025\"><a href=\"#L3025\">3025</a></th><td>\u00a0 that 0.1 will have to be 0.1f if it's a float, and some other</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3026\"><a href=\"#L3026\">3026</a></th><td>\u00a0 tidbits like that.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3027\"><a href=\"#L3027\">3027</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3028\"><a href=\"#L3028\">3028</a></th><td>- the \"examples\" folder for sketches is read-only. \"save as\" of an</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3029\"><a href=\"#L3029\">3029</a></th><td>\u00a0 example won't save it inside the examples folder.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3030\"><a href=\"#L3030\">3030</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096295037;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3031\"><a href=\"#L3031\">3031</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3032\"><a href=\"#L3032\">3032</a></th><td>- read-only sketches (i.e. from a CDROM) are now handled properly.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3033\"><a href=\"#L3033\">3033</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3034\"><a href=\"#L3034\">3034</a></th><td>- you can save sketches anywhere you want. and there's a preferences</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3035\"><a href=\"#L3035\">3035</a></th><td>\u00a0 dialog that lets you set the location of your sketchbook. that</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3036\"><a href=\"#L3036\">3036</a></th><td>\u00a0 annoying \"sketchbook/default\" thing is no more. in preferences, </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3037\"><a href=\"#L3037\">3037</a></th><td>\u00a0 you can also set whether processing should ask your for the file</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3038\"><a href=\"#L3038\">3038</a></th><td>\u00a0 location &amp; name for each new sketch, or if you just want the old</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3039\"><a href=\"#L3039\">3039</a></th><td>\u00a0 behavior (automatically created sketch named sketch_yymmdd).</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3040\"><a href=\"#L3040\">3040</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096295141;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3041\"><a href=\"#L3041\">3041</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3042\"><a href=\"#L3042\">3042</a></th><td>- holding down 'shift' and hitting the 'new' button will do the</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3043\"><a href=\"#L3043\">3043</a></th><td>\u00a0 opposite behavior for \"new sketch\" (i.e. if \"prompt for sketch name\"</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3044\"><a href=\"#L3044\">3044</a></th><td>\u00a0 is selected in preferences, it won't prompt, and vice versa).</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3045\"><a href=\"#L3045\">3045</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3046\"><a href=\"#L3046\">3046</a></th><td>- preferences and sketchbook are now stored in: </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3047\"><a href=\"#L3047\">3047</a></th><td>\u00a0 macosx: /Users / yourusername / Documents / Processing</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3048\"><a href=\"#L3048\">3048</a></th><td>\u00a0 windows: Documents and Settings / yourusername / My Documents / Processing</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3049\"><a href=\"#L3049\">3049</a></th><td>\u00a0 linux: home directory -&gt; .processing </td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3050\"><a href=\"#L3050\">3050</a></th><td>\u00a0 you can change the sketchbook location, but this folder will</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3051\"><a href=\"#L3051\">3051</a></th><td>\u00a0 continue to be used to store preferences.txt and other files that</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3052\"><a href=\"#L3052\">3052</a></th><td>\u00a0 may be needed in the future.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3053\"><a href=\"#L3053\">3053</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3054\"><a href=\"#L3054\">3054</a></th><td>- a default template can be used for exporting applets. copy</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3055\"><a href=\"#L3055\">3055</a></th><td>\u00a0 applet.html from processing's \"lib\" folder to your sketch's folder,</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3056\"><a href=\"#L3056\">3056</a></th><td>\u00a0 and modify it to your heart's content. each time you re-export, your</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3057\"><a href=\"#L3057\">3057</a></th><td>\u00a0 html file will be used instead of the standard one.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3058\"><a href=\"#L3058\">3058</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096297644;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3059\"><a href=\"#L3059\">3059</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096297669;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3060\"><a href=\"#L3060\">3060</a></th><td>\u00a0 http://processing.org/discourse/yabb/YaBB.cgi?board=BugFixes;action=display;num=1096297787;start=0</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3061\"><a href=\"#L3061\">3061</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3062\"><a href=\"#L3062\">3062</a></th><td>- javascript support is now handled by saying</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3063\"><a href=\"#L3063\">3063</a></th><td>\u00a0 \"Import Library -&gt; javascript\"</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3064\"><a href=\"#L3064\">3064</a></th><td></td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3065\"><a href=\"#L3065\">3065</a></th><td>- for advanced users, what was formerly called 'bagel' is now in</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3066\"><a href=\"#L3066\">3066</a></th><td>\u00a0 package processing.core. we'll refer to this as \"core\", and the</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3067\"><a href=\"#L3067\">3067</a></th><td>\u00a0 files can be found in lib/core.jar of the processing folder. no more</td></tr><tr><th href=\"#L3277\">3277</a></th><td>\u00a0 split(someString, \", \") will split on any number of comma or space</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3278\"><a href=\"#L3278\">3278</a></th><td>\u00a0 chars in between (sort of a regexp but not really).</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3279\"><a href=\"#L3279\">3279</a></th><td>\u00a0 to split on commas and any amount of whitespace between, use:</td></tr><tr><th linefeed, carriage return, etc) plus the unicode</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3284\"><a href=\"#L3284\">3284</a></th><td>\u00a0 \"non breaking space\" char.</td></tr><tr><th id=\"L3285\"><a
